utility_component_template = {
	key = "SPACEBORNE_COMBAT_COMPUTER_SWARM_BIONIC"
	size = small
	icon = "GFX_ship_part_computer_role_swarm_bionic"
	icon_frame = 1
	power = -20
	resources = {
		category = ship_components
		cost = {
			alloys = 10
			sr_dark_matter = 1
			acot_sr_dark_energy = 1
		}
	}
	class_restriction = { shipclass_military }
	size_restriction = {
		amoeba_small
		droid_miner
		droid_corvette
		small_crystal_ship
		mercenary_corvette
		void_cloud
		space_tiyanki
		droid_destroyer
		medium_crystal_ship
		mercenary_destroyer
		migrant_destroyer
		merchant_destroyer
	}
	component_set = "combat_computers"
	ship_behavior = "swarm"
	prerequisites = { "tech_dm_combat_computer" }
	upgrades_to = "SPACEBORNE_COMBAT_COMPUTER_AE_OFFENSIVE"
	
	modifier = {
		ship_evasion_mult = 0.25
	}
	ship_modifier = {
		ship_fire_rate_mult = 0.20
	}
	
	ai_weight = {
		weight = 205
		modifier = {
			factor = 0
			has_monthly_income = {
				resource = sr_dark_matter
				value <= 2
			}
			has_resource = {
				type = sr_dark_matter
				amount <= 5
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0
			has_resource = {
				type = acot_sr_dark_energy
				amount <= 5
			}
			has_monthly_income = {
				resource = acot_sr_dark_energy
				value <= 2
			}
		}
	}
}
